<div class="fc-item__content">
<div class="fc-item__header">
<h1 class="fc-item__title"><a href="https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2017/oct/27/release-jfk-files-fbi-warning-oswald-soviet-missile-fears" class="fc-item__link" data-link-name="article"><span class="fc-item__kicker">John F Kennedy</span> <span class="u-faux-block-link__cta fc-item__headline"> <span class="js-headline-text">Release of files reveals FBI warning on Oswald and Soviets' missile fears</span></span> </a></h1>
</div>
<div class="fc-item__standfirst">
Publication of 3,000 documents sheds more light on response to assassination of US president  but so far no smoking gun
</div>
